Dry Needling : What to Expect  
in Joondalup & Yanchep
======================================================

![applying acupuncture needle](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/applying-acupuncture-needle.jpg)

Dry needling is a technique that targets specific muscles and trigger points. It involves inserting a fine needle into affected areas of soft tissue, which may assist in reducing muscular tightness and discomfort.

After the treatment, [your practitioner](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 will assess the area for changes in muscle tone and mobility. It’s generally advised to rest for a few hours after your session. Strenuous physical activity, including gym workouts, may not be recommended immediately following treatment.

Potential Effects and Considerations
------------------------------------

Dry needling is one of several techniques used to manage musculoskeletal issues. Some individuals report temporary improvements in symptoms such as muscular tightness or localised discomfort. However, outcomes can vary and are dependent on several factors, including the nature of the condition and individual response.

![Needles on back](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/acupuncture-needles-in-back-wide.jpg)

Suitability and Safety
----------------------

Dry needling may not be appropriate for everyone. It is typically not recommended for:

*   Individuals with certain blood disorders
*   People with a history of fainting
*   Those with a significant fear of needles
*   Young children, due to difficulty staying still for the procedure

Your practitioner will assess your individual circumstances to determine whether dry needling is suitable for you.

Risks and Side Effects
----------------------

As with any procedure involving needles, there are potential risks. These may include:

*   Bruising
*   Temporary soreness or tenderness
*   In rare cases, more serious complications (which your practitioner will discuss with you)

Any concerns or medical history will be reviewed prior to treatment to help ensure safety.

Is It Right for You?
--------------------

Dry needling may be one option to consider as part of a broader musculoskeletal care plan. Its effectiveness varies between individuals. A comprehensive assessment is required to determine whether this technique is appropriate for your specific needs.

Frequently Asked Questions
--------------------------

[How does dry needling differ from traditional acupuncture?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/dry-needling/#toggle-1)

While both use similar tools, dry needling and acupuncture are based on different principles. Acupuncture is rooted in traditional Chinese medicine, focusing on restoring the body’s energy balance. Dry needling, as used in a chiropractic or musculoskeletal context, involves inserting fine needles into myofascial trigger points to assist in reducing muscle tension and improving function.

[What can I expect after a session?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/dry-needling/#toggle-2)

Some individuals may experience mild soreness, tenderness or bruising at the needle sites, which typically resolves within a few days. Most people are able to continue with their daily activities following a session.

[Are there any reasons dry needling may not be suitable?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/dry-needling/#toggle-3)

Dry needling may not be recommended for individuals with certain medical conditions such as bleeding disorders, active infections, or open wounds. Additional care is taken for individuals with allergies, delayed wound healing, or concerns related to needles. A full health history and assessment will be conducted to determine if this technique is appropriate for you.

[How soon might I notice changes?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/dry-needling/#toggle-4)

Responses to treatment vary. Some people report feeling a change soon after their session, while for others it may take a few treatments to notice an effect. Your chiropractor will monitor your progress and adjust your care plan accordingly.

Booking an Appointment
----------------------

If you’re interested in learning more about dry needling and whether it’s suitable for you, please contact [our practice](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 to arrange a consultation.  
[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

Endonasal Cranial Correction (ECC™) in Yanchep
==============================================

![](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/2013/11/headache-glasses.jpg)Endonasal Cranial Correction (ECC™) is a gentle manual technique that supports the natural alignment and movement of the cranial bones and surrounding structures of the head and neck.

Whole-Body Connection
---------------------

Unlike approaches that focus solely on the spine, ECC™ recognises the important relationship between the cranial system, posture, and overall structural balance.

At our practice, [Dr Matt (Principal Chiropractor](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/dr-matt-coxall/)
) takes a whole-body approach to care. When bones in the body, particularly within the skull, shift in ways the body cannot self-correct, it may influence comfort, posture, and function in other areas.

Some people choose to explore ECC™ to support concerns such as tension headaches, sinus pressure, jaw discomfort, or postural imbalance.

What to Expect During ECC™
--------------------------

During an ECC™ session, a small, soft balloon is gently inserted into the nasal passage and briefly inflated to encourage improved cranial movement.

This technique is performed as part of the [Advanced BioStructural Correction (ABC™)](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/advanced-biostructural-correction/)
 approach to care.

Areas ECC™ May Support
----------------------

![](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/closeup-young-woman-tooth-ache.jpg)ECC™ is used as an adjunct to chiropractic care and may assist with:

*   Nasal or sinus congestion
*   Facial tension or asymmetry
*   [Head or neck tension](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/neck-pain/)
    
*   Jaw discomfort
*   [Postural imbalance](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/poor-posture/)
     and spinal alignment
*   A sense of restricted breathing through the nose

As with all manual therapies, individual experiences and outcomes can vary.

Frequently Asked Questions
--------------------------

**Does ECC™ hurt?**

Most people find ECC™ comfortable. You may feel brief pressure in the nasal area during the procedure, but it usually subsides quickly.

**How long does an ECC™ session take?**

A session typically lasts only a few minutes and is performed as part of a broader chiropractic visit.

**Is ECC™ suitable for everyone?**

Your chiropractor will assess your health history and comfort level before recommending ECC™ to ensure it is appropriate for you.

Book a Consultation

 is trained in both [Advanced BioStructural Correction](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/advanced-biostructural-correction/)
 and Endonasal Cranial Correction, and tailors each plan to suit individual needs and goals.

If you would like to learn whether ECC™ may be suitable for you, contact our team at [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 to schedule a consultation.

We will take the time to discuss your goals, perform an assessment, and outline your options clearly.

Care for Headaches and Migraines in Joondalup & Yanchep
=======================================================

[Our practice](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 offers patient-centred care that focuses on understanding your individual health concerns, including headaches and migraines. Living with recurring headaches can be challenging, and we’re here to support you in exploring non-pharmaceutical options that may help you manage your symptoms.

![Woman holding hands to temples](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/woman-holding-hands-to-head-400.jpg)Understanding Headaches
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Headaches are among the most commonly reported types of discomfort.

There are various forms, including:

*   Tension headaches, often related to stress or muscle tension
*   Cervicogenic headaches, which may be linked to structures in the neck
*   Migraines, a more complex type of headache that can involve sensitivity to light, sound, and movement

Identifying potential contributing factors, such as posture, screen time, or stress, is an important step in managing headache symptoms.

Contributing Lifestyle Factors
------------------------------

Prolonged periods at a desk, poor posture, and high levels of stress may contribute to discomfort in the neck and shoulders, which some individuals associate with headaches. Adjusting certain lifestyle factors, such as workstation setup and sleep habits, may assist in managing these symptoms.

How Chiropractic Care Could Help
--------------------------------

[Chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 may help some people manage headache-related symptoms. Through manual techniques aimed at improving joint function and reducing muscular tension, some patients may report relief from certain types of headaches, particularly those related to neck tension or posture.

Each person responds differently, and outcomes can vary. Chiropractic care is not a cure for headaches or migraines, but it may be part of a broader approach to managing symptoms for some individuals.

What to Expect
--------------

Your [first visit](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/)
 will include a thorough consultation and physical examination to better understand your health history and current concerns. If chiropractic care is appropriate for your situation, your chiropractor will explain the recommended approach and may perform an adjustment tailored to your needs.

We also provide guidance on posture, ergonomics, and other lifestyle factors that may support your overall wellbeing.

Important Information
---------------------

As with any healthcare treatment, chiropractic care carries potential risks. [Your chiropractor](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 will explain these to you and ensure any care provided is appropriate for your needs and preferences. Individual outcomes vary, and we encourage you to ask questions and make informed decisions about your care.

Book an Appointment
-------------------

Contact [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 today to schedule a consultation with a member of our team. We’re here to help you explore natural ways to manage your health.  
[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

_**Disclaimer:** Chiropractic care focuses on musculoskeletal health. Any treatment or advice provided is based on your individual presentation and may vary from person to person. Chiropractic care is not a replacement for medical treatment. If your condition falls outside our scope, we will refer you to an appropriate healthcare provider._

Support for Hip Discomfort and Movement Concerns in Joondalup & Yanchep
=======================================================================

[Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 provides personalised [chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 that is informed by current evidence. We take the time to understand your individual needs and circumstances, offering care and general lifestyle guidance aimed at supporting your overall wellbeing.

![Man with hip pain](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/man-with-hip-pain-flipped.jpg)Understanding Hip Discomfort
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Many people experience discomfort in the hip or pelvic region, which may be influenced by daily posture, activity levels, or muscle and joint function. In some cases, this may be accompanied by [lower back discomfort](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/lower-back-pain-and-sciatica/)
. These issues may affect one or both hips and can vary in intensity and duration.

You might notice discomfort when walking, running, or standing for extended periods. Rotational movements or certain postures may also increase tension around the hip area. Footwear, posture, and repetitive movements are among the factors that can contribute to or aggravate these symptoms.

When to Seek Help
-----------------

If your discomfort persists, restricts movement, or interferes with your daily activities, it may be helpful to consult a qualified health professional. Chiropractors are trained to assess musculoskeletal function and may provide care aimed at improving joint mobility and supporting overall function.

What Chiropractic Care May Involve
----------------------------------

[Chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 may include manual techniques such as gentle joint mobilisation or soft tissue approaches, depending on your individual presentation. The goal is to support your musculoskeletal health and function, in alignment with your needs and goals.

We may also discuss factors such as posture, daily habits, or workstation ergonomics to help reduce strain and support your comfort and movement.

Please note that chiropractic care is not a treatment for specific medical conditions or diseases, and any recommendations made are based on your individual assessment and needs.

Your First Visit
----------------

During your [initial consultation](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/)
, [your chiropractor](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 will take a detailed health history and conduct a physical assessment to understand your concerns and determine if chiropractic care is appropriate for you. Based on this, a personalised care plan will be discussed, which may include advice on self-care and strategies to support your overall musculoskeletal health.

Book an Appointment
-------------------

We offer both early and late appointments to suit your schedule. Contact our friendly team today to book an [initial consultation](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/)
 and learn more about how we may be able to assist with your movement and joint concerns.  
[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

How Chiropractic Care Can Help With Your Shoulder Pain From Swimming
====================================================================

Published on February 15, 2022

![person swimming in a pool](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/person-swimming.jpg)Swimming is a great sport for everyone. Whether you are still young or even up to your 80s and beyond, you can benefit from swimming. No matter someone’s background or level of experience at swimming, they can still benefit from it.

Many health benefits come with swimming, as stated in an article by Better Health Channel, such as a normal heart rate, building endurance, improving muscle strength, and maintaining cardiovascular fitness.

Since this sport engages our whole body to navigate the water, we can easily provide a full-body workout since you’ve been using head-to-toe for swimming. Indeed, swimming has a good impact on both our physical and mental health.

On the contrary, our bodies can also get worn out by excessive swimming and repetitive motion, which can cause pain. Since swimming mainly requires the shoulders to get through the water, they are more prone to pain than other joints and muscles used for the said sport.

Almost every swimmer has experienced pain in their shoulders more than once in their lives, and good treatment options for relieving discomfort have been offered to help others recover from the pain they got from swimming.

One of the most effective treatment options for shoulder pain is chiropractic care. [Chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 is performed using spinal manipulations to relieve pain in someone’s joints and muscles. These adjustments will increase blood flow and nerve conductivity to the affected areas where the pain is present.

More so, it can also be used in other body conditions which can cause pain such as neck pain, back pain, headaches and migraines, knee pain, and even hip pain.

Understanding Shoulder Pain with the Help of Chiropractic Care
--------------------------------------------------------------

Our shoulders are used as flippers when we swim through the water, and it is evident that it’s one of the most used parts of the body when it comes to swimming; that is why shoulder pain is a common condition among many swimmers.

Here, we will dive deeper into shoulder pain and how chiropractic care could help.

The most common condition that causes shoulder pain is a swimmer’s shoulder which affects almost 80% of swimmers, according to statistics provided by Science Daily on youth swimmers. Swimmer’s shoulder occurs due to overuse and repetitive motion within the shoulders, which can cause the tendons to get inflamed and press on nearby bones, muscles, and even other tendons.

Sometimes, swimmers with a swimmer’s shoulder wouldn’t notice the symptoms at first, but it would gradually develop and become worse the longer they swim and stay in the water. Swimmers with this kind of shoulder pain can have a reduced range of motion and increased joint laxity compared to the other shoulder that isn’t damaged at all. If not brought to attention, a swimmer’s shoulder can limit the range of motion in the shoulders.

Another Type of Shoulder Pain
-----------------------------

![person holding their shoulder in pain](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/young-adult-holding-shoulder-in-pain-sq-400.jpg)The other type of shoulder pain is shoulder bursitis, which happens when the bursa, a fluid-filled sac that protects the tendons and reduces friction within the shoulder, becomes inflamed. This type of shoulder pain is also caused by overuse and may trigger pain, discomfort, weakness, and stiffness in the shoulder.

Pain from shoulder bursitis can be felt suddenly, and stiffness is one of the most common symptoms of this condition. People suffering from shoulder bursitis can also report pain going worse during nighttime, as their shoulders get pressed when they lay down their mattresses.

According to chiropracticcare.today, these shoulder conditions that cause shoulder pain are treatable and manageable by chiropractic care. One way to relieve discomfort from these conditions is by chiropractic adjustments, which use the hands of your chiropractor to apply a sudden yet controlled force on an affected joint. In this way, the body’s range of motion will increase, improve physical function, and address joint fixations.

Another way to treat shoulder pain with chiropractic care is through therapeutic exercises, which your chiropractor has specially designed for your type of shoulder pain. Since shoulder pain can cause muscle spasms within the shoulder, soft tissue therapy is also performed.

Before conducting any exercises or chiropractic adjustments, you may have to receive a comprehensive physical examination first, so chiropractors know your history and accurately diagnose your condition. Then, they’ll give you adjustments to the problem area by doing exercises and treating them based on the severity of your pain.

After your chiropractic sessions, you’ll receive suggestions from your chiropractor about modifying your swimming training plan to help reduce the risk of a shoulder injury and speed up recovery.

Swimming does wonders for our body, but sometimes, overusing our bodies for swimming can cause us pain. Even if you are just a beginner attending swimming lessons or a competitive swimmer with years of experience; we cannot impossibly avoid pain completely. However, with the help of chiropractic care, we can help recover from the pain and continue with swimming.

Our team at [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 is a group of experts passionate about providing quality chiropractic care for patients who want to start being active again in life. We are dedicated to helping people move freely without worrying about pain as we practice a lifestyle of fitness, mobility, and nutrition. Our holistic approach drives us to understand your needs and improve your wellbeing. If shoulder pain has been bothering you for such a time, we are happy to assist you in your recovery.

Has Shoulder Pain Been Bothering You?
-------------------------------------

The team at Biotune Chiropractic is here to help! Contact us today to get started.  
[CONTACT US »](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

How Dry Needling Can Relieve Pain and Improve Muscle Function Naturally
=======================================================================

Published on June 12, 2025

![dry needling back](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/acupuncture-hands-sq-400.jpg)Muscle pain can take a toll on your day, whether it’s post-workout soreness, office-chair stiffness, or tension that just won’t budge. [Dry needling offers a natural, hands-on approach that focuses directly on trigger points in the muscles](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/dry-needling/)
. It is a drug-free way to reduce pain and improve mobility without relying on medication.

This modern, evidence-informed technique is becoming a trusted tool among chiropractors and other healthcare providers across Joondalup. It supports the body’s own healing response without the need for medications.

What Makes Dry Needling Different?
----------------------------------

Dry needling involves inserting fine, sterile needles into tight or knotted muscles (called trigger points) to release tension and restore normal muscle function. While it may look similar to acupuncture, the techniques are completely different. Dry needling targets muscle tissue, not energy flow.

How It Works Inside the Muscle
------------------------------

The moment the needle reaches a trigger point, you might feel a twitch – this is just the muscle reacting to the release. The result? Better blood flow, less muscle tension, and nerve stimulation that supports healing from the inside out.

Who Might Benefit?
------------------

Dry needling may help with conditions like:

*   Neck tension and headaches
*   Lower back strain and sciatica
*   Shoulder pain and impingement
*   Elbow pain (tennis/golfer’s elbow)
*   Heel and foot pain, like plantar fasciitis

It’s a practical option for active individuals, desk workers, or anyone managing chronic discomfort.

What You’ll Feel in a Session
-----------------------------

We’ll start with a chat and a gentle assessment. During the session, you might feel a quick prick or a twitch sensation as the needle finds the right spot. The needles are sterile and single-use. They stay in for a few minutes and are then removed to check the muscle’s response.

Our team is trained in anatomy and precise technique. We take the time to assess your needs before starting any care. Sessions are brief, and we tailor the number of visits to your needs. A bit of post-session soreness is normal; you may want to skip the gym that day and allow your body to recover.

Why Patients Choose Biotune Chiropractic for Their Care
-------------------------------------------------------

[We take a personal approach to our patients’ wellbeing](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/)
. Whether you’re a weekend warrior, desk-bound office worker, or dealing with long-term discomfort, we’ll tailor our care to your goals and support your health with hands-on, thoughtful care.

Ready to see if this approach could help you? Book a consultation today and feel the difference for yourself.

How Will You Invest in Your Spine this World Spine Day?
=======================================================

Published on October 15, 2025

![world spine day](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/General-Wellness20-240x300.jpg)On 16 October, [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 will join millions of people worldwide in recognising **World Spine Day 2025**. This annual public health initiative highlights the importance of spinal wellbeing and the impact that spinal issues have on communities worldwide.

Why World Spine Day Matters
---------------------------

According to the World Health Organisation (WHO), more than 600 million people are affected by low back pain, with numbers continuing to rise. World Spine Day brings much-needed attention to this challenge, while encouraging individuals to take an active role in caring for their spine. The campaign also supports advocacy for improved access to spinal healthcare resources where they are needed most.

The Theme: Invest in Your Spine
-------------------------------

The 2025 theme, _Invest in Your Spine_, reminds us that spinal health is a lifelong priority. Investment can be as simple as making small daily choices that support your body or planning occasional check-ins with a [qualified health professional](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
. Each action contributes to building mobility, strength, and long-term resilience in daily life.

Everyday Habits that Support Spinal Health
------------------------------------------

There are many simple steps you can take to support a healthier spine, including:

*   Staying active with at least 30 minutes of daily movement
*   Using ergonomic seating and maintaining good posture
*   Taking time to stretch throughout the day
*   Limiting long periods on mobile devices
*   Eating a balanced diet and keeping hydrated
*   Aiming for seven to eight hours of quality sleep
*   Taking regular breaks from sitting or repetitive activities

These practices, when built into your daily routine, may help support spinal health and contribute to overall wellbeing over time.

Join Us This World Spine Day
----------------------------

This World Spine Day, Biotune Chiropractic encourages individuals and families to take small, positive steps that support their spinal health. For more information or to schedule an appointment, please contact our team today!

[Book an Appointment](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

Biotune Chiropractic  
Web Accessibility Statement
==================================================

We are committed to making the Biotune Chiropractic website available to all users, including those with disabilities. As part of this commitment, we are continually improving our website to ensure we provide equal access to all of our users.

* * *

General
-------

Biotune Chiropractic has invested a significant amount of resources to help ensure that our website is made easier to use and more accessible to people with special needs, including those with visual, hearing, cognitive and motor impairments. We are updating our site regularly to make it as accessible as possible.

Accessibility
-------------

Biotune Chiropractic makes available the [UserWay Website Accessibility Widget](https://userway.org/ "Free Website Accessibility Widget")
 that is powered by a dedicated accessibility server. The software allows Biotune Chiropractic to improve its compliance with the Web Content Accessibility Guidelines (WCAG 2.0).

Our team also uses tools such as, WAVE by WebAIM, Web Accessibility by Monsido, and other color contrast analyzers to ensure the best experience possible for all visitors.

The site is being designed to meet Level AA Success Criteria of the Web Content Accessibility Guidelines 2.0 to the greatest extent feasible.

![userway icon](https://doc.vortala.com/global/images/userway.png)

Enabling the Accessibility Menu on Biotune Chiropractic
-------------------------------------------------------

The accessibility menu can be enabled by clicking the accessibility menu icon that appears on the corner of the page. After triggering the accessibility menu, please wait a moment for the accessibility menu to load in its entirety.

Disclaimer
----------

Biotune Chiropractic continues its efforts to constantly improve the accessibility of its site and services in the belief that it is our collective moral obligation to allow seamless, accessible and unhindered use also for those of us with disabilities.

Despite our efforts to make all pages and content fully accessible, some content may not have yet been fully adapted to the strictest accessibility standards. This may be a result of not having found or identified the most appropriate technological solution.

We make reasonable efforts to ensure that PDF files posted on our website are accessible.

Work to Do
----------

We are in the process of improving our Alternative Text (Alt Text) for images so that only images that present valuable information include meaningful alternative text for screenreader users; any decorative images will not include alt text.

We’re Here For You
------------------

If you are experiencing difficulty with any content, require assistance with any part of our website, or would like to request any information in an accessible alternative format, please [contact us](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)
 at **(08) 9301 2229** during normal business hours and we will be happy to assist.

Accessibility Problem or Suggestion
-----------------------------------

If you have any concerns or suggestions regarding the accessibility of the Biotune Chiropractic website, please [use this form to provide your feedback](https://vortala.formstack.com/forms/web_accessibility_feedback&url=https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au)
. We value your feedback and will consider all suggestions as we evaluate ways to accommodate all users of our website and our overall accessibility policies.

* * *

**Updated:** January 2018

Privacy Policy
==============

This Privacy Policy applies to the Biotune Chiropractic website. The Biotune Chiropractic website is provided for information and educational purposes and may contain links to other sites. Once you enter another website (whether through an advertisement, service, or content link), be aware that Biotune Chiropractic is not responsible for the privacy practices of such other sites. We encourage you to look for and review the privacy statements of each and every website that you visit.

We believe that transparency is the key to any healthy relationship. At Biotune Chiropractic, we’re all about healthy. We appreciate that you are trusting us with information that is important to you, and we want to be transparent about how we use it. Here we describe the privacy practices for our website and you will learn about the data we collect, how we use it, the controls we give you over your information, and the measures we take to keep it safe.

Information We Collect and How We Use Information
-------------------------------------------------

* * *

We collect the following personal information from you on the Biotune Chiropractic website forms.

*   First and Last name
*   Email address
*   Phone number

By entering this information, you are providing personal information that will be used by Biotune Chiropractic for the sole purpose of scheduling your appointment or returning your contact request.

If you choose to enroll as a subscriber of our website or subscribe to our blog, you will receive recurring practice newsletters, announcements and occasional promotional information via email. These emails will be of a general nature and will in no way disclose your unique health characteristics.

To subscribe to our website, we need certain contact information, such as your name and email address. We may also store any provided demographic information (such as gender, birth date and address), but it is not required. You can unsubscribe from the newsletters or any of our emails by simply clicking on the “unsubscribe” link at the bottom of our emails; you will be immediately unsubscribed.

If you wish to stop receiving text messages from us, reply STOP to any text message sent from us. Instructions are provided on the first message sent to the contact.

Passive Information We Collect

Like many other websites, we also automatically collect and log other non-identifying information when you interact with the Biotune Chiropractic website:

**Device data.** We collect data from the device and application you use to access the Biotune Chiropractic website, such as your Internet protocol (IP) addresses, operating system, device type, browser type and timestamps.

**Usage data.** We collect usage data that may include which Biotune Chiropractic webpages you visit, what you click on, when you performed those actions, and so on. Emails sent by Biotune Chiropractic collect information about who opened those emails and clicked on links in them. We do this to measure the performance of the Biotune Chiropractic email messaging and to monitor and improve email deliverability and open rates.

Disclosure of Information
-------------------------

* * *

We do not sell, trade, or otherwise transfer your personally identifiable information to outside parties.

We respect your privacy and are committed to protecting your personal information. Any mobile opt-in information or personally identifiable data collected will not be shared, sold, traded, or transferred to any third parties or affiliates for marketing or promotional purposes.

We will only release personally identifiable information to comply with valid legal requirements, such as search warrants, subpoenas, or court orders. In the event that we are legally compelled to disclose your information to a third party, we will attempt to notify you unless doing so would violate the law or court order.

* * *

At the time you choose to enroll as a subscriber of our website or any time thereafter, you can choose to opt-out of receiving emails from us by simply clicking on the “unsubscribe” link at the bottom of our emails; you will be immediately unsubscribed.

You may ask us at any time for information about any personal data we hold about you, or ask us to correct or delete that information.  to start this process. If you need further assistance regarding your rights, please contact our office, and we will consider your request in accordance with applicable laws.

To the extent required under applicable law, and subject to our rights to limit or deny access/disclosure under applicable law, you have the following rights in your Personal Data. You may exercise your rights by contacting us at the address below.

**Access:** You may receive a list of your Personal Data that we process to the extent required and permitted by law.

**Rectification:** You may correct any Personal Data that we hold about you to the extent required and permitted by law.

**Deletion:** To the extent required by applicable law, you may request that we delete your Personal Data from our database.

Jaw Pain Care in Joondalup and Yanchep
======================================

At [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
, we provide professional care for individuals experiencing jaw discomfort, using a whole-body approach that considers factors such as neck posture, upper back alignment, and muscle tension. Our focus is on supporting musculoskeletal function and promoting comfort around the jaw and surrounding areas.

What Is the Temporomandibular Joint (TMJ)?
------------------------------------------

The temporomandibular joint (TMJ) connects the lower jaw (mandible) to the skull (temporal bone). Cushioned by small discs, this joint allows a wide range of motion for actions such as opening and closing the mouth, chewing, and speaking.

Common Causes and Symptoms of Jaw Pain
--------------------------------------

![](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/severe-mouth-pain-sq-300.jpg)Jaw discomfort can arise from a variety of factors, including:

*   muscle tension
*   teeth grinding or clenching (bruxism)
*   stress
*   [posture-related strain](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/poor-posture/)
    
*   fall or direct impact to the jaw or face
*   sports injury
*   extended mouth opening during dental procedures
*   side effects of certain diets or medications.

Symptoms can include pain around the jaw joint or temple, neck discomfort, headaches, dizziness, ear fullness, or clicking and popping sounds when opening or closing the mouth.

Jaw Pain Assessment and Diagnosis
---------------------------------

Before recommending any care, [our chiropractors](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 perform a thorough assessment of your jaw and related structures.

This may include discussing your symptoms and their duration, reviewing previous care, and evaluating lifestyle factors such as stress, sleep, diet, and posture. Jaw movement, muscle tension, and joint function are also assessed, along with how neck function and spinal alignment may influence the jaw.

This comprehensive assessment helps us understand the range of factors contributing to your discomfort.

Our Approach to Jaw Pain Care
-----------------------------

Our approach combines manual therapies, exercises, and whole-body guidance to support jaw comfort and function.

Care options may include:

*   Manual techniques to support jaw and neck movement
*   [Soft tissue therapy](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/soft-tissue-therapy/)
     such as massage, myofascial release, or [dry needling](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/dry-needling/)
     to address muscle tension
*   Exercise guidance to improve jaw posture, range of motion, and coordination
*   Lifestyle advice on stress, posture, and, if appropriate, consultation with dental professionals for bite assessment or splints

What to Expect During a Visit
-----------------------------

Your [first visit](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/)
 includes an assessment of jaw and cervical spine function, followed by gentle manual and soft tissue techniques to support movement and comfort. You may also receive home exercises and advice to help manage discomfort and encourage long-term jaw health.

Need Jaw Pain Support in Joondalup and Yanchep?
-----------------------------------------------

If you are experiencing jaw discomfort, our team can provide a thorough assessment and supportive care plan.

Our goal is to help you manage symptoms and promote comfort in your daily activities.

[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

_Disclaimer: Chiropractic care focuses on musculoskeletal health. Any treatment or advice provided is based on your individual presentation and may vary from person to person. Chiropractic care is not a replacement for medical treatment. If your condition falls outside our scope, we will refer you to an appropriate healthcare provider.

![Woman grabbing jaw.](https://doc.vortala.com/global/images/jaw-tension-feature.jpg)

Jaw Tension and Wellness: What Teeth Clenching Might Be Telling You
===================================================================

Waking up with a tight jaw or sore temples? Noticing yourself clenching your teeth during the day? Jaw tension is more common than many people realise – and it may be your body’s way of trying to tell you something: You’re stressed!

**The Link Between Stress and the Jaw**

The jaw is one of the areas in the body where stress often shows up. Clenching or grinding, especially at night, can put extra pressure on the muscles around the face, neck, and shoulders. Some people feel the effects as headaches or general discomfort in the upper back. If you’ve ever found yourself gritting your teeth while concentrating or driving, you’re not alone.

**Posture Plays a Part**

Poor posture, particularly when sitting at a desk or looking down at a phone, can contribute to jaw tension by altering the alignment of the head and neck. A forward head position may increase pressure on the muscles supporting your jaw. Becoming more aware of how you sit or stand throughout the day can help relieve some of that load. Even small shifts, like adjusting your monitor height or taking movement breaks, can make a difference.

**Gentle Habits That May Help**

If you’re noticing tension, simple steps like jaw relaxation exercises, breathing techniques, or using a warm compress at night may provide relief. Reducing screen time before bed and checking in with your posture during the day can also help manage strain.

Wondering if your lifestyle might be contributing to jaw tension? Our team is happy to chat – we’re here with practical, posture-friendly tips to support your everyday comfort.

Convenient Chiropractic Appointments  
to Suit Your Schedule
------------------------------------------------------------

Knee Pain Support in Joondalup & Yanchep
========================================

Every day at [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
, we see individuals with a range of musculoskeletal concerns, including knee pain. [Our chiropractors](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 are trained in various manual techniques and remain informed on current developments in musculoskeletal healthcare.

Although [chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 is commonly associated with back and neck issues, it may also assist with managing certain types of musculoskeletal knee discomfort. If your symptoms relate to joint or movement dysfunction, chiropractic care may form part of a broader approach to managing your condition.

![Man with knee pain](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/running-knee-pain-sq-400.jpg)Understanding Knee Discomfort
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Knee discomfort can arise from various causes, including sporting incidents, age-related changes, or increased load on the lower limbs. Sometimes, discomfort in the knee may also be linked to movement patterns or tension in other parts of the body.

When to Seek Support
--------------------

If you’re unsure whether your knee symptoms warrant further assessment, some signs that might indicate a need for professional evaluation include:

*   Discomfort when rotating or bending the knee
*   Stiffness, especially in the morning or cold weather
*   Pain at the front or inside of the knee joint
*   Difficulty with certain activities, such as walking or running for extended periods

Footwear and repetitive strain may also contribute to symptoms. A musculoskeletal assessment can help determine potential contributing factors.

How Chiropractic Care May Be Involved
-------------------------------------

Chiropractors focus on the assessment and management of the musculoskeletal system. Where appropriate, this may include gentle manual techniques aimed at improving joint function and addressing muscle tension.

If areas of restricted movement or altered biomechanics are identified, chiropractic care may help to manage symptoms and support overall function. We also offer advice on posture, movement strategies, and ergonomics to complement hands-on care.

Please note that chiropractic treatment is not a cure for knee pain, and outcomes vary depending on the individual. Where necessary, we may refer you to another healthcare provider for further investigation or co-management.

Your First Visit
----------------

Your [initial consultation](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/)
 includes a detailed health history and musculoskeletal assessment. If chiropractic care is considered suitable for your condition, we will discuss a management plan tailored to your needs.

This may involve manual therapy, exercises, or lifestyle advice, depending on your situation. We take a whole-body approach, considering how other areas may impact knee function.

Book an Appointment
-------------------

We offer flexible appointment times to fit your schedule. Contact us today to arrange a consultation and musculoskeletal assessment.  
[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

_**Disclaimer:** Chiropractic care focuses on musculoskeletal health. Any treatment or advice provided is based on your individual presentation and may vary from person to person. Chiropractic care is not a replacement for medical treatment. If your condition falls outside our scope, we will refer you to an appropriate healthcare provider._  
![divider](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/divider1.png)

Lower Back Pain Care in Joondalup & Yanchep
===========================================

At [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
, we offer [chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 that aims to support individuals experiencing musculoskeletal issues, including lower back discomfort. [Our team of chiropractors](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 is dedicated to assessing your individual needs and providing care that may assist in the management of your symptoms.

![Woman sitting on bed with hands on lower back](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/woman-on-bed-with-back-pain-sq-400.jpg)Understanding Lower Back Pain
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Lower back pain is one of the most commonly reported health concerns in Australia. According to the Australian Institute of Health and Welfare, around 70-90% of people will experience lower back pain at some point in their lives. The Australian Bureau of Statistics also estimates that approximately 16% of Australians live with back-related issues.

Lower back pain can be influenced by various factors, such as injury, posture, or repetitive movements. Some people may experience localised tenderness, while others might notice discomfort that radiates into the hips or legs. In some cases, episodes of lower back pain may resolve on their own, but for others, professional care may help manage ongoing or recurring symptoms.

Common Triggers
---------------

Certain activities and positions may aggravate lower back discomfort. These may include:

*   Sitting or standing for long periods
*   Sudden movements or lifting
*   Prolonged time in one posture, such as driving or working at a desk
*   Pre-existing conditions, such as disc-related issues, which may contribute to pain or stiffness

Every individual’s experience is different, and a thorough assessment is essential to determine contributing factors.

How Chiropractic Care May Help
------------------------------

[Chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 involves manual techniques, such as spinal adjustments or mobilisations, which aim to improve joint mobility and support musculoskeletal function. Some individuals with lower back pain report relief or improved movement following chiropractic care.

We begin with a comprehensive evaluation, including a detailed history and physical examination. This process helps us determine whether chiropractic care may be appropriate for your specific situation.

If we believe you may benefit from chiropractic care, we’ll develop a tailored plan that aligns with your needs. If chiropractic care is not suitable, we’ll refer you to another healthcare professional.

Your Individual Care Plan
-------------------------

Your chiropractor may provide recommendations to support your recovery, which could include:

*   Postural advice
*   Modifications to your workstation or sleeping positions
*   Movement and stretching suggestions tailored to your lifestyle

These recommendations are designed to support your overall wellbeing and assist in managing symptoms.

Convenient Appointment Times
----------------------------

We understand that our patients lead busy lives. That’s why we offer early and late appointments to help you access care at a time that works for you. Contact our [practice](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 today to request an appointment.  
[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

_**Disclaimer:** Chiropractic care focuses on musculoskeletal health. Any treatment or advice provided is based on your individual presentation and may vary from person to person. Chiropractic care is not a replacement for medical treatment. If your condition falls outside our scope, we will refer you to an appropriate healthcare provider._  
![divider](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/divider1.png)

Move Better, Work Better: Workspace Week 20-26 October 2025
===========================================================

Published on October 20, 2025

**![workspace week](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/workspace-week-sq-300x300.jpg)Workspace Week (20-26 October)** is a national initiative led by the Australian Chiropractors Association. It aligns with Safe Work Australia’s Australian Work Health and Safety (WHS) Strategy 2023-2033, which focuses on creating safe and healthy workspaces for all Australians. This year, the spotlight is on taking simple, practical steps that can reduce strain, boost energy, and help you stay focused during the day.

Why Your Workspace Matters
--------------------------

Musculoskeletal conditions are the #1 work health and safety issue affecting Australian workers, with [neck](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/neck-pain/)
 and [back pain](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/lower-back-pain-and-sciatica/)
 among the most common concerns. Around 7.3 million Australians (29%) live with chronic musculoskeletal conditions, and these cost the economy an estimated $55.1 billion annually.

Poor ergonomics can contribute to stiffness, fatigue, and discomfort, which makes work harder than it needs to be. The theme of Workspace Week is a timely reminder that prevention is the best protection. By making small, thoughtful adjustments, you can take proactive steps to support your body throughout the workday.

Simple Strategies to Try
------------------------

A healthier workspace doesn’t require an overhaul – just mindful changes:

*   Check that your screen is at eye level
*   Keep your feet flat on the floor
*   Take regular movement breaks to stretch or walk
*   Stay mindful of your posture throughout the day

Even these small adjustments can help reduce unnecessary strain and support focus and productivity.

Access Helpful Resources
------------------------

To help Australians make informed choices, the Australian Chiropractors Association has prepared fact sheets and checklists on topics such as sitting, standing, and lifting and bending correctly. These resources are filled with simple, practical advice that can be applied at home or in the office.

[Download the Fact Sheets and find additional information here](https://www.chiro.org.au/campaigns/workspace-week/)

Ready to Put These Tips Into Action?
------------------------------------

Making small changes to your daily setup is a smart starting point. If you’ve noticed ongoing tension in your back, neck, or shoulders, a chiropractor can assess your situation and offer tailored strategies to improve comfort and mobility.

Workspace Week is the perfect reminder to take charge of your habits and invest in long-term wellbeing. Don’t wait until discomfort slows you down – make changes today and feel the difference a healthier workspace can bring.

[Book an Appointment](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

Support for Neck Pain in Joondalup & Yanchep
============================================

[Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 is committed to providing whole-body [chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 with a focus on patient-centred outcomes. Our goal is to support your health and wellbeing with professional, evidence-informed care tailored to your individual needs.

![Woman sitting at desk with neck pain](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/woman-at-desk-with-neck-pain-sq-400.jpg)Understanding the Source of Neck Discomfort
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

People of all ages can experience neck pain, which may be related to a wide range of causes. Some individuals report localised discomfort, while others experience symptoms that may extend into the shoulders or arms. Headaches may also occur in certain cases, depending on the underlying contributing factors.

Common factors associated with neck discomfort include:

*   Whiplash or minor injuries
*   Prolonged sitting or desk work
*   Poor posture
*   Sleeping in an awkward position

Possible Effects of Neck Pain
-----------------------------

Neck pain may be accompanied by reduced movement, stiffness, muscle tenderness, or sensations such as tingling or numbness in the neck, shoulders, arms or hands. These effects can vary based on the nature and cause of the discomfort. Identifying contributing factors is an important step in developing a management approach.

How We Approach Care
--------------------

[Our chiropractors](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 provide manual therapy, including spinal adjustments, aimed at improving joint function and reducing associated symptoms. When certain joints are not moving as well as they should, this may contribute to local inflammation or muscular tension. Chiropractic care may assist in managing these symptoms by addressing joint restrictions and supporting musculoskeletal function.

Before any care is provided, your chiropractor will perform a thorough consultation, including a physical assessment and a review of your medical history. Based on this evaluation, we will discuss whether chiropractic care is suitable for your presentation and outline a recommended management plan.

Supporting Your Recovery
------------------------

In addition to in-practice care, we offer advice and strategies that may help support your recovery and overall wellbeing. For example, if your lifestyle includes extended periods of desk work, we can offer guidance on workstation setup and posture to help reduce physical strain. Our recommendations are tailored to your individual circumstances and aligned with your personal goals.

Your Personalised Management Plan
---------------------------------

Each person is different, and so is each management plan. If chiropractic care is considered appropriate for your situation, we’ll outline a plan that reflects your needs, preferences, and health objectives. Our practices use a combination of traditional and modern chiropractic techniques, and our team is committed to delivering care with professionalism and integrity.

Get in Touch
------------

We welcome the opportunity to meet with you and explore whether chiropractic care may be a suitable option for managing your neck discomfort. Contact our friendly team today to book your [initial consultation](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/)
. We offer flexible appointment times, including early and late hours, to accommodate your schedule.  
[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

Chiropractic care is not a replacement for medical treatment. If your condition falls outside our scope, we will refer you to an appropriate healthcare provider._

Frequently Asked Questions
--------------------------

[What should I wear to my appointment?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/#toggle-1)

We recommend wearing comfortable, loose-fitting clothing. However, whatever you arrive in, our team will work with you to ensure your comfort during the visit.

[Are chiropractic adjustments safe?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/#toggle-2)

Chiropractic adjustments are generally considered safe when performed by a registered chiropractor. As with any healthcare treatment, there can be some risks, which your chiropractor will discuss with you before proceeding.

[Why is there a clicking sound during an adjustment?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/#toggle-3)

A clicking or popping sound can occur when a gas bubble is released within the joint space during an adjustment. This is a normal and common occurrence. Some people report feeling more relaxed or mobile afterward, though individual experiences can vary.

[Why might adjustments be recommended?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/#toggle-4)

Every person’s body and lifestyle are different. Certain habits, such as prolonged sitting, repetitive tasks, or physical strain, can contribute to joint or muscle discomfort. Chiropractic care aims to support joint function and mobility where appropriate.

[Will I receive treatment at the first visit?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/#toggle-5)

In most cases, treatment can begin during your first visit. However, your chiropractor will first complete a thorough assessment to ensure treatment is suitable and safe. If additional tests or referrals are needed, these will be discussed with you.

[Will I need X-rays?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/#toggle-6)

Most people do not require X-rays. A diagnosis and treatment plan can often be developed through a detailed history and physical examination. If imaging is needed, it can be arranged and bulk billed where appropriate.

[Can I use my private health insurance?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/#toggle-7)

Yes. We have TYRO available, allowing you to claim directly through your private health insurance provider (if chiropractic is included in your cover).

[Does chiropractic care hurt?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/#toggle-8)

Most chiropractic adjustments are not painful. Some muscle techniques may feel firm, but your chiropractor will always tailor care to your comfort level and discuss what to expect beforehand.

[How do I get to Biotune Chiropractic?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/#toggle-9)

Our Biotune Joondalup practice is located at Unit 4B, 1 Wise Street. Street parking is located at the shopfront and also available at Lakeside Shopping Centre nearby, public transport is accessible within walking distance.

Our Biotune Yanchep practice is located at 1/99 Lindsay Beach Boulevard, within a six-lot, single-story commercial building that offers a range of professional services. There’s street-front parking available, as well as additional parking at the rear. A large multidisciplinary medical practice is located nearby.

[Want to know more or make an appointment?](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/#toggle-10)

Feel free to contact our friendly team, we’re happy to answer your questions or help you arrange a time to come in.

Osteoarthritis Care in Joondalup & Yanchep
==========================================

[Our chiropractors](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 at [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 offer natural healthcare that considers your whole body, from head to toe. One common condition we often see is osteoarthritis, the most prevalent form of arthritis worldwide.

What Is Osteoarthritis?
-----------------------

![Older smiling woman outdoors](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/senior-woman-outdoors-smiling-sq-400.jpg)Osteoarthritis is a joint condition that occurs when the protective cartilage at the ends of bones gradually wears down over time. It can affect any joint but is most frequently found in the [hips](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/hip-and-lower-limb/)
, spine, hands, and [knees](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/knee-pain/)
. People with osteoarthritis often experience joint pain, stiffness, and reduced mobility.

While the joint changes caused by osteoarthritis cannot be reversed, symptom management is possible, helping you maintain a better quality of life.

Common Symptoms of Osteoarthritis
---------------------------------

Osteoarthritis usually develops gradually and may worsen over time. Symptoms can include:

*   A grating or grinding sensation in the joint
*   Reduced mobility and flexibility
*   Joint swelling and tenderness
*   Pain and stiffness
*   Numbness or discomfort in nearby areas

Symptoms often affect one side of the body more than the other and can impact daily activities and work over time.

Factors That May Worsen Osteoarthritis Symptoms
-----------------------------------------------

Certain activities or situations, such as prolonged sitting during long flights, drives, or at a desk, may increase discomfort. Pre-existing injuries or changes in weather can also influence symptoms.

How Chiropractic Care May Help
------------------------------

After a thorough evaluation, your chiropractor will discuss a personalised care plan tailored to your specific condition and needs.

[Chiropractic adjustments](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 aim to improve joint movement and support musculoskeletal function, which may help reduce discomfort and improve mobility. Soft tissue therapies can complement this by addressing muscles and connective tissues, potentially assisting with symptom relief.

In addition, your chiropractor can provide practical lifestyle advice, including workstation setup and sleep habits, tailored to your individual circumstances to help manage your symptoms.

Important Information
---------------------

Chiropractic care does not cure osteoarthritis or reverse joint damage, but may help you manage symptoms and support your overall musculoskeletal health.

Ready to Take the Next Step?
----------------------------

Contact us today to book your [initial consultation](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/)
. We offer flexible appointment times to suit your schedule and look forward to helping you manage your osteoarthritis symptoms with personalised care.

[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

_**Disclaimer:** Chiropractic care focuses on musculoskeletal health. Any treatment or advice provided is based on your individual presentation and may vary from person to person. Chiropractic care is not a replacement for medical treatment. If your condition falls outside our scope, we will refer you to an appropriate healthcare provider._  
![divider](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/divider1.png)

Chiropractic Assessments for Infants in Joondalup & Yanchep
===========================================================

![Adjusting baby's back](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/infant-adjustment-on-spine-h.jpg)Caring for your baby’s physical development is essential, especially during the early stages of life. At [our practice](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
, [Dr Matt Coxall (Principal Chiropractor)](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/dr-matt-coxall/)
 offers gentle chiropractic assessments focused on identifying musculoskeletal issues that may be affecting your baby’s comfort or movement. Dr Matt is available at both our Joondalup and Yanchep practices.

A Gentle, Age-Specific Approach
-------------------------------

A baby’s spine and nervous system are delicate and continue to develop rapidly in the first year of life. Sometimes, events such as the birthing process can place physical stress on an infant’s body, which may affect their musculoskeletal system.

Dr Matt uses gentle techniques, often involving light touch, to assess your baby’s spine, joints, and posture. Any hands-on care is carefully adapted for infants, using very minimal pressure, similar to checking the ripeness of a piece of fruit.

Why Parents Seek a Musculoskeletal Assessment
---------------------------------------------

Some parents choose to bring their baby in for a chiropractic assessment when they notice signs of possible musculoskeletal discomfort, such as:

*   Difficulty turning the head in one direction
*   Asymmetrical movement or posture
*   Seeming uncomfortable in certain positions
*   General unsettled behaviour that appears related to movement

It’s important to note that chiropractic care is not a treatment for medical conditions such as colic, reflux, digestive issues, or developmental delays. However, if musculoskeletal factors are contributing to your child’s discomfort or movement patterns, chiropractic care may form part of a broader support approach.

![Tiny baby](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/brand-new-baby-holding-finger-wide.jpg)

Our Approach to Evidence-Informed Care
--------------------------------------

[Dr Matt](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/dr-matt-coxall/)
 is experienced in working within a multi-disciplinary care model and may recommend co-management with other healthcare providers, such as paediatricians, lactation consultants, or maternal health nurses, where appropriate. Our priority is to provide safe, evidence-informed care tailored to your child’s individual needs.

All care decisions are made in consultation with parents or guardians, based on a thorough clinical assessment and informed consent.

Important Information for Parents
---------------------------------

Chiropractic care for infants is focused on assessing and supporting the musculoskeletal system. If you have concerns about your baby’s health, such as feeding difficulties, growth concerns, or developmental milestones, it is important to consult a qualified medical professional.

Book an Appointment
-------------------

Help your little one get off to a healthy start in life. Contact [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 today to schedule an appointment.

[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

*   [BOOK APPOINTMENT](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)
    
*   [google social button](https://maps.google.com/?cid=8457868835080355708)
    [facebook social button](https://www.facebook.com/biotunechiropractic/)
    [instagram social button](https://www.instagram.com/biotunechiropractic/?hl=en)

Care for Plantar Fasciitis in Joondalup & Yanchep
=================================================

At [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
, we provide [chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 that supports whole-body wellbeing. While chiropractic is often associated with spinal health, many people seek our care for a variety of musculoskeletal issues. One condition some patients inquire about is plantar fasciitis, a common source of foot and heel discomfort.

![Woman with pain in her foot](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/woman-with-foot-pain.jpg)What Is Plantar Fasciitis?
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Plantar fasciitis involves irritation or inflammation of the plantar fascia, a band of tissue that runs along the bottom of the foot. It’s often associated with heel pain that may feel worse in the morning or after periods of rest. Some individuals also notice discomfort when flexing the foot or toes upwards. A tight Achilles tendon may contribute to increased tension in the affected area.

Recognising the Signs
---------------------

Common signs of plantar fasciitis can include:

*   Sharp or aching pain in the heel or foot, especially when taking the first steps after rest
*   Discomfort that may improve with gentle movement
*   In some cases, sensations such as tingling, radiating discomfort, or mild swelling

It’s essential to consult a healthcare professional for an accurate diagnosis, as other conditions can cause similar symptoms.

Supporting Foot and Biomechanical Health
----------------------------------------

[Chiropractors](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 are trained to assess the musculoskeletal system and may use manual techniques to address joint function, muscle tension, and body mechanics. While chiropractic care is not a treatment for plantar fasciitis specifically, some individuals with foot or lower limb concerns choose to explore chiropractic care as part of their broader health management.

Our approach may include:

*   Assessing overall posture and movement patterns
*   Addressing areas of joint restriction or muscle tension that could contribute to mechanical strain
*   Offering general advice on lifestyle habits, footwear, and ergonomic setup where relevant

Care recommendations are tailored to your specific needs and preferences. If appropriate, we may also suggest working alongside other healthcare providers such as podiatrists or physiotherapists.

What to Expect During Your Visit
--------------------------------

Your [first appointment](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/)
 will involve a thorough health history and physical examination. If chiropractic care is appropriate for your case, we will clearly explain your options and any recommendations. Care decisions are always made with your informed consent.

Flexible Appointment Options
----------------------------

We understand that your schedule can be busy, which is why we offer extended opening hours to accommodate your needs. Our aim is to provide timely and respectful care in a professional and supportive environment.

Contact Us
----------

If you’re experiencing foot or heel discomfort and are wondering whether [chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 may be suitable as part of your management, please contact our team. We’re happy to answer your questions or arrange a time for an initial assessment.  
[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

_**Disclaimer:** Chiropractic care focuses on musculoskeletal health. Any treatment or advice provided is based on your individual presentation and may vary from person to person. Chiropractic care is not a replacement for medical treatment. If your condition falls outside our scope, we will refer you to an appropriate healthcare provider._

Support for Poor Posture in Joondalup & Yanchep
===============================================

![Man and woman walking outdoors at sunset](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/couple-walking-at-sunset-sq-400.jpg)[Our team](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 at [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 is committed to supporting your overall wellbeing. [Chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 may help manage symptoms associated with musculoskeletal conditions. In today’s digital age, many people spend extended time using mobile devices, computers, or tablets, which can contribute to poor posture across all age groups.

How Poor Posture Develops
-------------------------

Poor posture can begin early in life and often results from daily activities and habits. Factors such as occupation, sports, and lifestyle can influence posture. Prolonged stress or strain, especially related to work, may increase the likelihood of experiencing discomfort in areas such as the neck and shoulders.

Poor posture often involves muscle imbalances, including muscles that become tight, shortened, lengthened, or weakened. Regardless of how posture issues develop, we have the skills and experience to assess and assist you.

Recognising Poor Posture
------------------------

Poor posture doesn’t always mean slumping forward. Since body types and alignment vary between individuals, what is correct posture for one person might differ for another. Poor posture often relates to musculoskeletal changes in the neck, upper back, and lower back.

Some common signs include:

*   A forward-tilted pelvis
*   Rounded shoulders
*   A protruding neck and chin
*   Hump at base of neck

Contributing Factors to Poor Posture
------------------------------------

A forward pelvis may be caused by an exaggerated curve in the lower back, which can affect the position of abdominal organs. Rounded shoulders and neck posture issues may result from excessive curvature in the neck or mid-back.

Extended periods of sitting, whether at a desk, during travel, or at home, may worsen posture. Taking regular breaks to move can help reduce this effect. Pre-existing injuries, such as a disc bulge, may make maintaining good posture more challenging.

Starting Your Care
------------------

Your care begins with a thorough examination. During your [first appointment](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/)
, we will conduct a physical evaluation and review your health history to understand your needs. If chiropractic care is appropriate, we can perform adjustments aimed at improving joint function, including areas that may be compensating for your symptoms.

We will also provide advice on lifestyle factors, such as sleeping habits and workstation ergonomics, to support your recovery.

Take the First Step
-------------------

Contact us today to arrange your [initial consultation](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/)
 for posture-related concerns. Our friendly team is available with early and late opening hours to suit your schedule.  
[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

_**Disclaimer:** Chiropractic care focuses on musculoskeletal health. Any treatment or advice provided is based on your individual presentation and may vary from person to person. Chiropractic care is not a replacement for medical treatment. If your condition falls outside our scope, we will refer you to an appropriate healthcare provider._

Pregnancy Chiropractic Care in Joondalup & Yanchep
==================================================

![webster technique adjustment](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/webster-technique-adjustment-h.jpg)Pregnancy is a time of significant physical and emotional change. Many women experience shifts in posture, joint mobility, and overall comfort as their bodies adapt. At Biotune Chiropractic we offer chiropractic care that is tailored to support your body’s natural changes during pregnancy.

Gentle Techniques for Expectant Mothers
---------------------------------------

As your pregnancy progresses, your body undergoes various changes that may influence your comfort and mobility. [Our chiropractors](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 use modified techniques that are gentle and considerate of these changes. We aim to support your musculoskeletal system throughout your prenatal journey, with care tailored to your stage of pregnancy and individual needs. We navigate around your changing body, focusing on making you as relaxed as possible.

![divider-dotted-1200](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/divider-dotted-1200.png)  
![Pregnant couple](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/pregnant-couple-relaxing-wide1.jpg)

Supporting You Throughout Your Pregnancy
----------------------------------------

Chiropractic care can be provided at all stages of pregnancy. During your [initial consultation](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/)
, we will take the time to understand your health history and any current concerns. Our approach is always personalised, and prenatal care is adjusted as needed throughout your pregnancy to support your comfort and mobility.

We use pregnancy-specific techniques where appropriate and avoid positions or adjustments that are not suitable during certain trimesters. Communication with your other healthcare providers is encouraged to ensure coordinated and appropriate care.

Postnatal Support for Your Comfort
----------------------------------

After childbirth, your body continues to change as it recovers and adapts to new physical demands. With your healthcare provider’s approval, chiropractic care may be used to support musculoskeletal function during the postnatal period. We also offer general advice on posture, gentle movement, and stretches that may help support your body during this time.

A Supportive Approach to Care
-----------------------------

Every pregnancy is unique. Our goal is to provide a safe and supportive environment where you feel heard and cared for. Chiropractic care at [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 is offered as a complementary therapy to help support your comfort and overall wellbeing throughout your pregnancy and into the postnatal period.

Book an Appointment
-------------------

If you’re pregnant and interested in supportive chiropractic care, contact our practice to book a consultation. Our caring and experienced chiropractors are here to provide care tailored to your individual needs.

**Disclaimer:** Chiropractic care is a complementary therapy and does not replace medical or obstetric care. Please consult your GP or obstetrician regarding any health concerns during pregnancy.

[https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/realistic-health-goals-that-you-can-actually-keep/](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/realistic-health-goals-that-you-can-actually-keep/)
