![Man drinking water.](https://doc.vortala.com/global/images/health%20goals%20you%20can%20keep%20feature.jpg)

Realistic Health Goals That You Can Actually Keep
=================================================

Health goals sound great on January 1…until life starts happening again. Work gets busy, sleep slips, routines get messy, and suddenly the plan feels impossible.

This year, consider choosing goals that are simple, flexible, and realistic—so you can keep them going long after the New Year buzz fades.

**Pick Goals That Fit Your Real Life**

A helpful goal is one that doesn’t require perfect conditions. Instead of aiming for a total routine overhaul, focus on habits you can repeat on your busiest week.

A good rule: if it feels “too much” to do daily, make it smaller until it feels doable.

**5 Health Goals You Can Reach (Without Burning Out)**

**1) Move a little every day**

This doesn’t have to be a workout. A short walk, stretching while the kettle boils, or a few mobility moves counts. Regular movement helps your body stay more comfortable and less tight.

**2) Improve one posture habit**

Choose just one. For example: keep your phone closer to eye level, adjust your chair support, or raise your laptop to reduce forward-head posture. Small changes here can reduce daily strain.

**3) Support your sleep routine**

Try one easy sleep anchor: a consistent wake-up time, less screen time before bed, or a wind-down routine that signals “off-duty” to your body.

**4) Drink more water (in a way that works)**

Instead of “8 glasses,” try linking water to habits you already do—one glass when you wake up, one with lunch, one mid-afternoon. Hydration supports your body’s natural balance and comfort.

**5) Add chiropractic care to your wellness plan  
**  
If your goal is to feel better in your body this year—less tightness, better movement, more ease day-to-day—chiropractic care can be a practical part of that plan. Many people find it helpful alongside movement, posture improvements, and better recovery habits.

**Keep It Simple**

The best health goals aren’t the most impressive ones—they’re the ones you can repeat. If you’d like support choosing a plan that fits your body and your schedule, reach out. We’re here with practical guidance and steady encouragement.

Sciatica Care in Joondalup & Yanchep
====================================

[Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 offers personalised care tailored to your individual musculoskeletal concerns. People often visit us with symptoms that may be related to sciatica, and we offer care that aims to support comfort, mobility, and function.

Understanding Sciatica-Like Symptoms
------------------------------------

![Chiropractor with female patient](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/dr-jill-mokrzycki-back-adjustment.png)Sciatica refers to irritation or compression of the sciatic nerve, which can cause discomfort that travels from the lower back into the leg. This discomfort may be due to a number of factors, including disc-related issues or muscular tension in the lower back or gluteal region. However, not all leg or back discomfort is due to sciatica, and a thorough assessment is needed to understand the cause.

Common Signs That May Be Associated with Sciatica
-------------------------------------------------

You may be experiencing the following:

*   Pain that travels into the leg, hip, buttock, thigh, or foot
*   Tingling or numbness in the lower extremities
*   Discomfort that may worsen with certain movements, such as bending or lifting
*   Increased symptoms during prolonged sitting

It’s important to note that symptoms vary between individuals, and not all people with nerve-related discomfort experience pain that extends to the foot.

What May Contribute to Sciatica-Like Discomfort
-----------------------------------------------

Various factors may aggravate sciatic nerve irritation, including prolonged sitting, physical strain, or repetitive movements. In some cases, pressure from surrounding muscles or structures may increase discomfort. The nature and progression of symptoms can depend on the underlying cause.

Chiropractic Support for Sciatica-Like Symptoms
-----------------------------------------------

[Chiropractors](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 use a variety of manual techniques to assess and manage musculoskeletal conditions. At our practice, we provide care that may assist with improving joint movement and relieving tension in surrounding muscles. This may contribute to reduced discomfort and improved function in some individuals.

Following a thorough consultation and physical examination, your chiropractor will discuss appropriate options for care based on your needs. We may also provide guidance on posture, ergonomics, and lifestyle factors that could support your recovery and general wellbeing.

Individualised Care Plans
-------------------------

Each person’s presentation is different. We focus on individualised care and work with you to determine the best approach. If [chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 is not suitable for your condition, we will advise you and may recommend referral to another health professional.

Schedule an Appointment
-----------------------

If you are experiencing symptoms that may relate to sciatica, contact our team to arrange a consultation. We provide flexible appointment times, including early mornings and evenings.  
[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

_**Disclaimer:** Chiropractic care focuses on musculoskeletal health. Any treatment or advice provided is based on your individual presentation and may vary from person to person. Chiropractic care is not a replacement for medical treatment. If your condition falls outside our scope, we will refer you to an appropriate healthcare provider._

Shoulder Discomfort and Mobility Support in Joondalup & Yanchep
===============================================================

[Our practice](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 takes a holistic, movement-based approach to musculoskeletal care. Here, [our chiropractors](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 assess your posture, joint function, and movement patterns to help support your physical wellbeing and reduce discomfort related to joint or soft tissue strain.

Understanding the Shoulder Joint
--------------------------------

![Man with shoulder pain](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/radiating-shoulder-pain-sq-400.jpg)The shoulder is a complex joint made up of muscles, tendons, and fluid-filled sacs called bursae. These bursae help reduce friction during movement. When irritated, they can contribute to feelings of discomfort, stiffness, or restricted range of motion.

Shoulder irritation can result from repetitive overhead movements, physical stress, or posture-related strain, which is commonly seen in people engaged in activities like manual labour or racquet sports.

Common Symptoms People May Experience
-------------------------------------

While shoulder discomfort can vary, people often report:

*   A dull ache in the front or side of the shoulder
*   Discomfort during or after activity
*   Increased pain at night
*   A feeling of weakness or reduced range of motion

If symptoms include redness, swelling, or a sudden loss of function, we recommend seeking medical attention to rule out more serious conditions.

How Chiropractic Care May Support You
-------------------------------------

[Our chiropractors](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 provide thorough assessments to understand your musculoskeletal presentation. If [chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 is considered appropriate, we may use manual techniques such as:

*   Gentle joint adjustments to address restricted movement
*   Soft tissue techniques to help reduce muscular tension
*   Postural or ergonomic advice tailored to your lifestyle

We do not diagnose or treat medical conditions, but some individuals report improvements in comfort and function when mechanical imbalances are addressed as part of a broader wellness approach.

Lifestyle Advice and Prevention
-------------------------------

We may also provide advice on sleep positions and pillow support, as well as desk and workstation ergonomics, and modifying repetitive activities to reduce shoulder strain. Our goal is to support your mobility and help reduce the risk of future flare-ups.

Discover Convenient, Personalised Care
--------------------------------------

We offer early and late appointment times to suit your schedule. Whether you’re looking to maintain your physical health or seeking support for a specific concern, our team is here to provide patient-centred care in a relaxed, professional environment.

Book your appointment at Biotune Chiropractic today to find out if chiropractic care may be suitable for your needs.  
[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

_**Disclaimer:** Chiropractic care focuses on musculoskeletal health. Any treatment or advice provided is based on your individual presentation and may vary from person to person. Chiropractic care is not a replacement for medical treatment. If your condition falls outside our scope, we will refer you to an appropriate healthcare provider._

Soft Tissue Therapy in Joondalup
================================

![](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/back-chiropractic-adjustment-h.jpeg)  
[Our chiropractors](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 use a comprehensive approach that combines [chiropractic adjustments](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 with a variety of soft tissue techniques. This integrated style of care may help ease discomfort, support recovery, and make everyday movement feel easier and more comfortable.

Soft tissue therapy focuses on the muscles, ligaments, and connective tissues that support your joints and spine. When combined with precise chiropractic adjustments, these methods can assist with flexibility, reduce tension, and encourage better body function.

Techniques We Use
-----------------

###   
Activator Method®

This technique uses a small handheld spring-loaded device called an Activator® to deliver a gentle impulse to specific areas of the spine or extremities. It is designed to support nervous system balance and musculoskeletal comfort.

###   
Diversified Technique

A widely used chiropractic approach, Diversified focuses on restoring spinal alignment and improving joint mobility. Through careful, hands-on adjustments, this technique aims to reduce stiffness and encourage natural movement.

###   
Dry Needling

[Dry needling](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/dry-needling/)
 involves inserting fine sterile needles into muscle trigger points to help relieve tension and improve muscle performance. It is often used to support recovery and mobility in people with musculoskeletal discomfort.

###   
Gua Sha

This soft tissue technique uses a smooth handheld tool to massage the muscles and fascia. Gua Sha helps improve circulation, ease tension, and may assist with discomfort linked to repetitive use.

###   
Sacro Occipital Technique (SOT®)

SOT® focuses on the connection between the pelvis, spine, and skull to encourage balance and comfort. Chiropractors use gentle adjustments and specialised supports to promote better alignment.

###   
Thompson Drop Table Technique

This method uses a specially designed chiropractic table with padded platforms that drop slightly during an adjustment. The light motion assists gentle spinal adjustments with minimal force.

###   
Trigger Point Therapy

Trigger Point Therapy targets tight or sensitive areas in the muscles. By applying sustained pressure with the fingers, thumbs, or elbows, these points are encouraged to release, which may help ease discomfort and restore flexibility.

Supporting Whole-Body Wellness
------------------------------

Each soft tissue and chiropractic technique is selected based on your individual needs, comfort level, and health goals. By combining these evidence-informed methods, our chiropractors aim to support your body’s natural ability to move and function at its best.

Schedule an appointment at [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 today and discover how our gentle techniques can support your everyday comfort and mobility.

[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

![divider](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/divider1.png)

Tennis Elbow Care in Joondalup & Yanchep
========================================

[Our practice](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 provides patient-centred care informed by current best practices in chiropractic and musculoskeletal health. If you’re experiencing elbow discomfort, we’ll take the time to understand your symptoms and determine whether [chiropractic care](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 may be suitable for your needs.

![Man holding elbow in pain](https://doc.vortala.com/static/uploads/9/files/man-in-plaid-holding-elbow-sq-400.jpg)What Is Tennis Elbow?
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tennis elbow, or lateral epicondylitis, is a condition that causes pain on the outer part of the elbow. It’s often related to repetitive wrist and arm movements that can place stress on the tendons of the forearm.

Common Symptoms may include:

*   Pain or tenderness on the outside of the elbow
*   Difficulty gripping or lifting objects
*   Discomfort when shaking hands or turning a doorknob
*   Weakness in the forearm
*   Pain that may radiate down to the wrist

Symptoms may worsen with activities such as typing, racquet sports, manual work, or lifting.

Can Chiropractic Care Help With Tennis Elbow?
---------------------------------------------

At your [first appointment](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/new-patients/)
, [our chiropractors](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)
 will conduct a thorough history and physical assessment. If your symptoms are consistent with tennis elbow and chiropractic care appears appropriate, we’ll discuss a care plan tailored to your needs.

We may use a combination of gentle manual techniques, soft tissue work to support surrounding areas, and advice on posture, ergonomics, and activity modification.

Our goal is to support your musculoskeletal health and movement. If your condition requires care outside our scope, we will refer you to the appropriate health professional.

A Whole-Body Approach
---------------------

Tennis elbow can be influenced by how the joints in your shoulder, neck, and wrist function. We assess the whole body to identify contributing factors and support overall biomechanics, which may help reduce strain on the affected area.

Lifestyle and Self-Care Advice
------------------------------

We’ll also offer practical advice that may help reduce symptoms and prevent recurrence, such as:

*   Ergonomic workstation setup
*   Posture tips
*   Sleep positioning and pillow selection
*   Activity modification strategies

Book a Consultation
-------------------

If you’re experiencing elbow discomfort or symptoms similar to tennis elbow, we’re here to help assess your condition. Contact [Biotune Chiropractic](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/about-us/)
 today to book an appointment.

We offer early and late appointments for your convenience.  
[CONTACT US](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/contact-us/)

_**Disclaimer:** Chiropractic care focuses on musculoskeletal health. Any treatment or advice provided is based on your individual presentation and may vary from person to person. Chiropractic care is not a replacement for medical treatment. If your condition falls outside our scope, we will refer you to an appropriate healthcare provider._

Collaborative Care

Chiropractor in Yanchep
=======================

![Dr Aneesh adjusting patients neck](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/Dr-Aneesh-adjusting-patients-neck.jpg)Biotune Chiropractic is proud to offer [chiropractic services](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/chiropractic-care/)
 at our northern most location in Yanchep and surrounding suburbs. Conveniently located in the heart of Yanchep our practice has supported the local community and surrounds with professional, patient-focused care for over five years.

Led by our experienced chiropractors [Dr Matt Coxall](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/dr-matt-coxall/)
 and [Dr Aneesh Manji](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/dr-aneesh-manji/)
, Biotune Yanchep is committed to providing tailored chiropractic care that supports your posture, spinal health, and overall well-being. The Yanchep practice upholds the same patient-focused approach as our Joondalup location, offering quality chiropractic care in a professional and welcoming environment.

[MEET THE TEAM](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/meet-the-team/)

Convenient Chiropractic Appointments to Suit Your Schedule
----------------------------------------------------------

Our practice offers both morning and evening appointments to make chiropractic care more accessible when you need it most. Same-day bookings and walk-ins are welcome. You do not need a referral from a GP to see our qualified chiropractors.

Our Approach: Advanced BioStructural Correction (ABC™)
------------------------------------------------------

At our Yanchep practice, we primarily use the chiropractic technique known as [Advanced BioStructural Correction (ABC™)](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/advanced-biostructural-correction/)
. This hands-on method is designed to address certain structural imbalances in the body. The aim is to support improved spinal alignment and overall posture.

Many people seek chiropractic care for a range of musculoskeletal concerns, including:

![Dr Coxall talking to patient](https://doc.vortala.com/childsites/uploads/2891/files/patient-with-dr-coxall.jpg)

*   [Poor posture](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/poor-posture/)
    
*   [Back](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/lower-back-pain-and-sciatica/)
     and [neck pain](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/neck-pain/)
    
*   [Headaches and tension](https://www.biotunechiropractic.com.au/headaches-and-migraines/)
    
*   Spinal misalignments

While responses to care can vary from person to person, some patients report feeling more comfortable or mobile after chiropractic adjustments. We always aim to provide care that is appropriate to your individual presentation and goals.

Postural Support Through Chiropractic Care
------------------------------------------

ABC™ is focused on supporting postural alignment and spinal mechanics. While posture plays a role in musculoskeletal function, it is one of many factors that may contribute to your overall sense of wellbeing. Our team is focused on helping you manage posture-related concerns with care that is tailored, considered, and based on current best practices.

Insurance and Payment Information
---------------------------------

Biotune Chiropractic Yanchep accepts a variety of payment methods and insurance options, including:

*   Private health insurance (with TYRO available)
*   Medicare referrals under the GP Chronic Condition Management Plan (GPCCMP)
*   Department of Veterans’ Affairs (DVA)

If you’re unsure about your coverage or entitlements, feel free to contact our team, we’re happy to assist with any questions you have.

## Document 65 — Your Nervous System 101: Understanding How Your Body Responds to Stress {#doc-65}

![Woman grabbing face.](https://doc.vortala.com/global/images/body-stress-feature.jpg)

Your Nervous System 101: Understanding How Your Body Responds to Stress
=======================================================================

Ever felt wired but exhausted? Or maybe you find it hard to relax even after a long day? That may have more to do with your nervous system than you think.

**Meet Your Two Modes**

Your body’s nervous system has two main settings: the sympathetic (commonly known as “fight or flight”) and the parasympathetic (“rest and digest”). The sympathetic system prepares you to respond to stress, while the parasympathetic helps you calm down and recover. Both are important, but spending too much time in a heightened state can lead to tension, poor sleep, or feeling on edge.

**Everyday Stress Adds Up**

Modern life tends to keep us in a go-go-go state. Whether it’s juggling work, family, or constant notifications, your nervous system can get stuck in overdrive. This might show up as jaw clenching, tight shoulders, shallow breathing, or trouble falling asleep. You may not even realise how tense you are until someone points it out!

**Simple Ways to Support Balance**

The good news? Small daily choices can support a more balanced nervous system. Gentle movement, deep breathing, and regular sleep patterns all help shift your body into a calmer state. Setting boundaries around screen time, creating a wind-down routine, or spending time outdoors are also useful ways to invite in more “rest and digest” moments.

**Tuning In Is Step One**

Your nervous system is always working in the background to keep you regulated. Learning how to recognise its signals – and support it with healthy habits – can lead to noticeable changes in how you feel physically and emotionally.

Not sure where to start? We’re here to help you tune in and feel more supported. Just reach out anytime for practical, personalised guidance.
